				<script type="text/javascript">
			$J( function() {
				BindAutoFlyoutEvents();

				var $Window = $J(window);
				var $Header = $J('#store_header');
				var $ResponsiveNavWindowShadeCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_ctn');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlay = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlayCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay_ctn');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlayBottom = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay_bottom');
				var $HeaderWrapper;
				$Window.on('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu', function() {
					var bUseSmallScreenMode = window.UseSmallScreenMode && window.UseSmallScreenMode();

											if ( !$HeaderWrapper )
							$HeaderWrapper = $Header.wrap( $J('<div/>', {'class': 'responsive_store_nav_ctn_spacer'} ) ).parent();

						if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
							$ResponsiveNavWindowShadeCtn.append( $Header );
						else
							$HeaderWrapper.append( $Header );


						if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
						{
							$Header.css( 'visibility', 'hidden' );
							$Header.show();

							var nStartingScrollPosition = $J('#store_header').height();
							if ( $Window.scrollTop() < nStartingScrollPosition )
								$Window.scrollTop( nStartingScrollPosition );

							$Header.css('visibility', 'visible');
						}
									} );
				
				window.setTimeout( function() { $J(window).trigger('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu'); }, 0 );

										var g_rgUserPreferences = {
							excluded_tags : [],
							excluded_content_descriptors : [3,4]						};
						
													g_rgUserPreferences['use_store_query'] = 1;
						
						g_rgUserPreferences['use_search_spellcheck'] = 1;
						g_rgUserPreferences['search_creators_and_tags'] = 1;

						if( $J('#searchform').length > 0 )
						{
							// default search support where the web page includes the search edit control
							EnableSearchSuggestions( $J('#searchform')[0].elements['term'], '1_5_9_', 'SG', 1, 'schinese', g_rgUserPreferences, '20236292' );
						}
						else 
						{
							// search support for the mobile client.  the mobile client has a native search edit control but relies on the web content to perform the query and show results
													}
				
				// make genre categories expand/collapse on mobile
				$J(document).on( 'click', '.popup_genre_expand_header', function ( event ) {
					if ( !UseSmallScreenMode() )
						return;

					event.preventDefault();
					var $Element = $J(this);
					var $Target = $J('.popup_genre_expand_content[data-genre-group=' + $Element.data('genre-group') + ']' );
					if ( $Element.data('group-expanded') )
					{
						$Target.slideUp();
						$Element.data( 'group-expanded', false );
					}
					else
					{
						$Target.slideDown();
						$Element.data( 'group-expanded', true );
					}
				});
			} );
		</script>

                                    <script type="text/javascript">
                                        $J( function() {
                                            var player = new HighlightPlayer( {
                                                elemPlayerArea: 'highlight_player_area',
                                                elemStrip: 'highlight_strip',
                                                elemStripScroll: 'highlight_strip_scroll',
                                                elemSlider: 'highlight_slider',
                                                rgScreenshotURLs: rgScreenshotURLs
                                            } );

                                            $J('#highlight_slider_right').click( function() {
                                                player.Transition( true );
                                            });
                                            $J('#highlight_slider_left').click( function() {
                                                player.TransitionBack( true );
                                            });

                                            
                                                // swipe gesture handling for the media carousel

                                                // TODO: We may want to move all of this to the player class so it has built in touch gesture support.
                                                // First testing here as part of new mobile ux.

                                                var k_nElementWidth = 120;
                                                var k_playerItemClassName = '.highlight_player_item';
                                                var g_nStripWidth = 960;
                                                var g_nMediaItems = player.m_elemPlayerArea.find( '.highlight_player_item' ).length;
                                                var g_TouchEventStart = null;

                                                // Handle left/right swipe on the media playback by moving forward or backward when the swipe completes
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchstart", function (event) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = event;
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchmove", function (event) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    var xdiff = Math.abs( g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX );
                                                    var ydiff = Math.abs( g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY );

                                                    // To reduce unintended page scroll during a horizontal swipe block the default handler when it looks like the user
                                                    // is in the process of performaing a horizontal scroll
                                                    if ( xdiff > ydiff && ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable ) )
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchend", function (eventEnd) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0] == undefined ||
                                                        typeof eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0] == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    var xdiff = g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX;
                                                    var ydiff = g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY;

                                                    // clear out the touch start event
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = null;

                                                    // ignore the swipe if it was short and could've been intended as a tap, or the
                                                    // direction was more vertical than horizontal
                                                    if ( Math.abs( xdiff ) < 20 || Math.abs( ydiff ) > Math.abs( xdiff ) )
                                                        return;

                                                    // we're handling this event
                                                    if ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable )
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                    // move forward or backward but don't wrap as that would be a jarring user experience
                                                    if ( xdiff > 0 )
                                                    {
                                                        var $NextItem = player.m_activeItem.next( k_playerItemClassName );
                                                        if ( $NextItem.length )
                                                            player.Transition( true );
                                                    }
                                                    else
                                                    {
                                                        var $NextItem = player.m_activeItem.prev( k_playerItemClassName );
                                                        if ( $NextItem.length )
                                                            player.TransitionBack( true );
                                                    }
                                                });

                                                // when the thumbnail strip is swiped move the strip at a granular level
                                                // so it feels active.  The active image does not update because when testing the code to
                                                // make it change the active element it seemed annoying
                                                var g_nSwipeStartingPosition = 0;
                                                var g_nMaxScroll = g_nMediaItems > 3 ? ( ( g_nMediaItems - 3 ) * k_nElementWidth ) : 0;

                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchstart", function (event) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = event;
                                                    g_nSwipeStartingPosition = parseInt( player.m_elemStripScroll.css( 'left' ) );

                                                    player.StopCycle();
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchmove", function (event) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    // To reduce unintended page scroll during a horizontal swipe block the default handler when it looks like the user
                                                    // is in the process of performaing a horizontal scroll
                                                    var xdiff = parseInt( event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX );
                                                    var ydiff = parseInt( event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY );
                                                    if ( Math.abs(ydiff) > Math.abs(xdiff) )
                                                        return;

                                                    // move the scroll strip without changing the selected item
                                                    var nNewScrollPosition = parseInt( g_nSwipeStartingPosition + xdiff );

                                                    // check that we don't scroll past the ends
                                                    if ( nNewScrollPosition > 0 )
                                                        nNewScrollPosition = 0;
                                                    else if ( nNewScrollPosition < (-1 * g_nMaxScroll) )
                                                        nNewScrollPosition = (-1 * g_nMaxScroll);

                                                    // set the new scroll position
                                                    player.m_elemStripScroll.css( 'left', nNewScrollPosition + 'px' );

                                                    // we're handling this event
                                                    if ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable )
                                                        event.preventDefault();
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchend", function (eventEnd) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = null;
                                                    g_nSwipeStartingPosition = 0;
                                                });

										
                                            if( window.location.hash )
                                            {
                                                var ssid = window.location.hash.substr(1);
                                                player.HighlightScreenshot(ssid);
                                            }
                                        } );
                                    </script>
                                                            </div>
                        					</div>
				</div>
				<div style="clear: both;"></div>
			</div>
			</div>

									<div class="game_page_autocollapse_ctn collapsed"><div data-panel="{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;PanelGroup&quot;}" id="aboutThisGame" class="game_page_autocollapse" style="max-height: 850px;">
						<div id="game_area_description" class="game_area_description">
							<h2>关于这款游戏</h2>
							<a href="https://store.steampowered.com/sale/2019_top_vr/" target="_blank" rel=""> <img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/877200/extras/ZeroCaliber_VRAwards_01_small.png?t=1690794363"> </a><br><br>Modding, cross-play PvP and the QoL update is LIVE!<h2 class="bb_tag">ABOUT THIS GAME</h2><br>Zero Caliber is the ultimate VR shooter with a full-blown single player/Co-op campaign (up to 4 players), cross-play PvP game modes and native mod support.<br>Rise through the ranks to unlock a wide variety of weapons and attachments, customize them, climb, jump, crouch, shoot, get to cover, reload, invite your friends, repeat - be prepared for a mind-blowingly immersive experience! <br><br><a href="https://steamcommunity.com/linkfilter/?url=https://springboardvr.com?game_verification=57f73140-5c47-11e9-8c45-959ed89ff02e" target="_blank" rel=" noopener"> Available for Arcades on SpringboardVR </a><h2 class="bb_tag">REALISTIC COMBAT SYSTEM - MOVE YOUR BODY TO FIGHT AND FIND COVER</h2><br>Handle, aim and reload your weapons with real-life movements! We modeled the in-game weapons based on their real-life counterparts paying extreme attention to detail. Each weapon has its unique reloading method that you have to learn and practice to fully master them. <br>If you fancy explosions, just grab a grenade and throw it at the enemy. After you pulled the pin of course.<br>Stay in the open for too long and you’re dead. Try to find cover instead, duck, crouch, sneak, peek around a corner, clear obstacles with real-life movements. Military combat isn’t all about shooting. Being aware of your surroundings, the terrain, and working together with your squadmates are all part of a successful mission. Don’t let your fellow soldiers down!<h2 class="bb_tag">REALISTIC WEAPONS - CUSTOMIZE YOUR FAVOURITE GUN</h2><br>Everyone has a unique playstyle. Is accuracy your thing? Put a laser sight on your assault rifle and take accurate shots in semi-automatic mode, or just grab a sniper rifle. Are you more of a shoot first, ask later type of person? Take a shotgun, or dual wield your machine guns in fully automatic firing mode. Be careful though, recoil can make your job really difficult! Combine your favourite gun with your favourite attachments on-the-fly to find out which variation suits you the most!<h2 class="bb_tag">THE STORY - DIVE INTO AN ENGAGING DYSTOPIAN ADVENTURE IN THE NOT TOO DISTANT FUTURE</h2> <br>Water is life. Someone should’ve made that clear before humanity started poisoning Earth with microplastics. Now water is death. People are fighting for drinkable water, for survival.<br>The military tried their best to keep order, but inevitably they got overwhelmed. That’s when mercenaries appeared.. then entire private armies.. and then when hope started to fade away came the religious cults. The most fearsome of all is a secretive organization worshipping Tlaloc, the aztec God of rain. The “Tlalokii”, as they call themselves. Their motto? “Join us or perish”. What is even worse, they know something that can change the fate of humanity.<br>Be part of this action-packed, story-driven VR adventure where you fight alongside your fellow soldiers trying to keep order… or what’s left of it anyway.<h2 class="bb_tag">MODDING</h2><br>Download community-made single player/co-op missions or PvP maps, or make your own in Unreal Engine through mod.io! <br>Modding guides: <a href="https://steamcommunity.com/linkfilter/?url=https://mod.io/g/zero-caliber/r" target="_blank" rel=" noopener">https://mod.io/g/zero-caliber/r</a><br>Direct assistance from the devs on Discord: <a href="https://steamcommunity.com/linkfilter/?url=http://discord.gg/xrealgames" target="_blank" rel=" noopener">http://discord.gg/xrealgames</a>  <br><br><strong>A constantly developing military VR FPS experience that will surely make you forget that you are in a video game!</strong>						</div>

									<div class="early_access_review tooltip" data-tooltip-text="该评测被撰写时，Zero Caliber VR 被标记为 Steam 抢先体验游戏">抢先体验版本评测</div>
				
													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary45733260_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：2018 年 11 月 10 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					作为第一个关于这个游戏的中文评测，我已经接触并游玩绝大多数优秀的vr射击游戏，arzoniasunshine通关并联机困难模式，onward美服频繁时期每天玩两到三局，pavlov vr最高美服dm模式击杀80人，评测这个游戏我也同样具有资质，我期待这个游戏已经两个月了，从它发布alpha宣传片到发布demo版本，我都很期待，试玩demo版本，demo版本只有靶场，正式版我等了一个月左右，今天发布，我立马下单购买，结果进游戏我就蒙蔽了，这和demo版本差不了多少，就三关任务模式，其他枪械还没解锁，还不能进靶场，游戏优化有很大问题，最低画质与最高画质帧数竟然相差不大，并且游戏画面极度不舒服，不如其他战争游戏那样有感觉，很流畅，这款游戏唯一的亮点就是对vr枪械游戏的一些细节的优化，比如原力拾起枪械，不需要伸手，自己飞过来，感觉很好，而且弹道已经各种物理效果针对新手来讲非常的友好，但是这仅仅就是其中几个亮点，其他都是喷点，ai傻逼到爆，画面刺眼，而且仍然不开放多人联机模式，希望有想购买游戏的朋友再等等吧，我已经吃亏了。					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

												<div class="num_reviews"><a href="https://steamcommunity.com/id/Chaneky/recommended/">153 篇评测</a></div>

			<div class="rightcol" id="ReviewContentsummary72535207_rightcol">
								<a href="https://steamcommunity.com/id/Chaneky/recommended/877200/" class="vote_header tooltip" data-tooltip-text="阅读完整评测">
					<div class="thumb">

										<img class="review_source tooltip" data-tooltip-text="产品是从 Steam 直接购买的" src="https://store.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/shared/images/userreviews/icon_review_steam.png">
					
					<div class="title ellipsis">推荐</div>
										<div class="hours ellipsis">
						总时数 11.0 小时												（评测时 7.9 小时）											</div>
									</a>
				
									<div class="early_access_review tooltip" data-tooltip-text="该评测被撰写时，Zero Caliber VR 被标记为 Steam 抢先体验游戏">抢先体验版本评测</div>
				
													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary72535207_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：2020 年 7 月 12 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					拟真向的VR射击游戏，做的挺好的。<br><br>拟真方面做的实在是不错，从枪械的配件搭配到枪械使用都很大程度上还原了真实枪械的操作。<br>但是，不能进行枪械的拆解，毕竟主要是个射击游戏。<br>还有个不够细节的地方就是，AR系列的枪械弹夹是直上直下的没问题，AK系列的弹夹真实情况下是先将弹夹前端放进去，再把后端往上卡进去，卸弹夹则是把弹夹往前推先将后端拔出在拔出整个弹夹，游戏很难做到这么细，只是给追求拟真感的玩家提个醒。<br><br>枪械种类比较丰富，有各种拉栓步枪，射手步枪，自动步枪，半自动手枪，盾牌和冲锋枪。提供了各种配件比如瞄准镜，握把，枪口和雷射进行混搭。<br><br>游戏里人物移动方式是用摇杆进行平移，讲实话，我第一次用这种方式移动之后，缓了两天，因为太晕了想吐，游戏可以通过自动遮挡周围视野提供舒适的移动模式，但是我觉得帮助实在不大，还是提供瞬移方式更好。<br>玩了几天之后，我其实也就不晕了。<br><br>游戏配置要求是比较高的，我开了中画质玩的，还算流畅，Ultra画质和High都只能40帧，VR视角的看到的游戏画质明显感觉是比之后电脑录象画面要好的，如果不是VR游戏中画质差不多比CS1.6强点的感觉吧，场景还行就是人物比较多边形。<br><br>我单人剧情8小时全打完了只有15级，然而很多自动步枪和狙击枪需要五六十级才能解锁，这不是离谱吗？！<br><br>游戏大厅有枪械库和靶场，除了肩膀感觉不到后座力，整个打枪感觉和和真实靶场的感觉还是挺像的。<br>游戏似乎更新了多人模式，但我还没试过。<br><br>这是我玩的第一款VR拟真射击游戏，总体感觉还是很好的，拟真度肯定是够的，就是枪械解锁慢并且配置要求高。					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

								<a href="https://steamcommunity.com/profiles/76561197998248112/recommended/877200/" class="vote_header tooltip" data-tooltip-text="阅读完整评测">

											</div>

										<img class="review_source tooltip" data-tooltip-text="产品是从 Steam 直接购买的" src="https://store.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/shared/images/userreviews/icon_review_steam.png">
					
					<div class="title ellipsis">不推荐</div>
										<div class="hours ellipsis">
						总时数 49.3 小时												（评测时 33.9 小时）											</div>
									</a>
				
									<div class="early_access_review tooltip" data-tooltip-text="该评测被撰写时，Zero Caliber VR 被标记为 Steam 抢先体验游戏">抢先体验版本评测</div>
				
													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary55873205_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：2019 年 10 月 29 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					虽然我曾经好评过，但对于现在这次隔了多年才更新的内容实在是非常不满意，这游戏早就应该脱离EA，但制作组好像完全没有放在心上。<br><br><b> 以下是目前游戏存在的问题： </b><br>1、多人联机的优化并没有解决，推出了PVP打得莫名其妙，体验非常糟糕。<br>2、需要更具游戏性的关卡设计。目前的关卡除了训练关和雪原爬塔之外，几乎没有需要用到攀爬功能的地方，这本应是对游戏性的提升，但是大部分到后面就是单纯的加速冲锋和射击，动作射击游戏丢失了本应作为卖点的动作部分，这是目前关卡设计不可取的。<br>3、收集品的引导。我做了全地图的收集品视频攻略并发到了<a class="bb_link" href="https://steamcommunity.com/linkfilter/?url=https://www.bilibili.com/video/av70993603/" target="_blank" rel=" noopener"> bilibili	</a>，每一个地图摸索一个小时到半个小时左右，<u> 最后还是没找到AK47的最后一个皮肤 </u>。对于设计方想要通过这个方式来增加玩家重复游玩的倾向是不行的，因为在逐个搜索一些不可能会去的角落或草丛的过程中，玩家的游戏节奏就会被完全打断，寻找过程中除了枯燥不会有任何游玩的快感，建议通过一些游玩门槛(如以XX武器爆头击杀XX人），以成就的方式来奖励玩家，而遍地藏枪的模式，就留给那些特殊的类似于“DEVP3T3”的特殊刻字武器和三点PEQ15激光瞄具这种彩蛋福利就够了。<br>4、开放的MOD支持但不支持创意工坊，虽然这样并没有太大问题，但选择了一个非常小众而且不够开放的第三方平台。<br>5、懒惰的更新内容和反复的跳票，mod支持和PVP这一部分本来会早一年上线，但是没想到会浪费这么长的时间去做这一点点的内容，新地图依旧缺乏地图互动，爬墙的功能依旧就是一个用不上的噱头。在制作组滥竽充数的时候，已经有许多优秀的射击类VR游戏诞生，现在的内容和玩点我已经不会首先推荐这款游戏了。					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

										<img class="review_source tooltip" data-tooltip-text="产品是从 Steam 直接购买的" src="https://store.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/shared/images/userreviews/icon_review_steam.png">
					
					<div class="title ellipsis">推荐</div>
										<div class="hours ellipsis">
						总时数 44.8 小时												（评测时 6.3 小时）											</div>
									</a>
				
									<div class="early_access_review tooltip" data-tooltip-text="该评测被撰写时，Zero Caliber VR 被标记为 Steam 抢先体验游戏">抢先体验版本评测</div>
				
													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary45742041_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：2018 年 11 月 10 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					写于2018.11.10 EA阶段（发售当日）<br>使用设备：Oculus Rift<br><br>个人感觉ZERO CALIBER是最接近于“VR版使命召唤”这一称号的VR FPS了。<br>游戏感觉介于基本是VR版CS的Pavlov VR和真实感很强的Onward之间。<br><br><div class="bb_h1">优点</div><br>最突出的是<b>物理引擎</b><br>这一点体现在武器部件和场景的互动，比如枪会撞到墙（不会像大多数VR游戏那样会穿过去），你可以把墙架在桌子上，也可以靠在墙上。枪和部件之间可以互动，可以像现实里的战术装填一样用AK的另一个弹夹“撞”掉打空的弹夹。（其实应该是用另一个弹夹去碰AK的换弹杠杆，但是不知道为什么，游戏里所有枪都可以这么做）敌人被击中时身体反应也更真实，看着对方被几发子弹的冲击力打翻，满足感十足。<br><br>你可以看到你自己的手臂，而不是像大多数VR游戏一样是一双<span class="bb_strike">小左小右</span>手悬在空中（这一点我个人感觉增强了代入感，尤其是在你一边奔跑一边射击时）<br><br>本作和制作组前作A-Tech Cybernetic VR是一样的引擎，画面在VR游戏里相当出众，当然对机器要求也更高，尤其是战役模式里人多的地方掉帧会十分明显，渲染距离也会多少有一些物体随着距离远近消失的情况（不过不是特别严重）<br><br><div class="bb_h1">缺点</div>（或是现阶段的不足）<br><br>因为是EA阶段，战役模式并没有做完（目前除去训练关和模拟战，剧情模式只有三关），流程中也有不少BUG，AI也很智障。<br><br>枪械上，枪声的感觉不算特别假但也不能说让人满意，不如说感觉很微妙。有些武器安不安消声器枪声没有区别；子弹快打完时的声音听着也有点怪（不是那种随着残弹数越少而越“脆”的感觉而是听上去像是你自己被震聋了一样枪声越来越小）。加装配件时有些配件的位置也感觉很怪。（后座力的感觉也更接近使命召唤的设定而不是男友）<br><br>目前多人模式服务器还不是很稳，而且只有合作模式<br><br>我个人感觉这是一部值得入手而且相当有潜力的VR射击游戏。<br>有兴趣可以下载试玩版体验。<br>期待日后的发展。					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

				<div class="posted">
					<div class="view_more"><a href="#" onclick="UserReviewShowMore('45742041', 'summary' ); return false;">展开阅读</a></div>

				</div>
